# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka Consumer Offset Commit to GroupCoordinator Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a consumer offset commit travels from KafkaConsumer.commitSync() to the __consumer_offsets topic in apache/kafka. Find Java source files implementing: commitSync(), ConsumerCoordinator.commitOffsetsSync(), GroupCoordinator.handleCommitOffsets(), and the offset log append.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

Perfect! I've successfully traced the Kafka consumer offset commit flow and created the comprehensive answer file. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary

The consumer offset commit travels through the following chain:

**Client Side (Synchronous Path):**
1. **KafkaConsumer.commitSync()** - Public API entry point
2. **ClassicKafkaConsumer.commitSync()** - Internal implementation
3. **ConsumerCoordinator.commitOffsetsSync()** - Coordinates the commit with retries
4. **ConsumerCoordinator.sendOffsetCommitRequest()** - Creates and sends OffsetCommitRequest

**Broker Side (Request Handling):**
5. **KafkaApis** (Scala) - Routes the request to GroupCoordinator
6. **GroupCoordinatorService.commitOffsets()** - Schedules write operation

**Coordinator State Machine:**
7. **GroupCoordinatorShard.commitOffset()** - Delegates to metadata manager
8. **OffsetMetadataManager.commitOffset()** - Validates and generates records

**Log Persistence:**
9. **GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.newOffsetCommitRecord()** - Creates CoordinatorRecord
10. **CoordinatorRuntime.scheduleWriteOperation()** - Batches records for writing
11. **CoordinatorPartitionWriter.append()** - Final append to __consumer_offsets topic

The answer has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with all relevant files, symbols, call chain details, and a comprehensive narrative explanation.

This also handles periodic offset commits\n500:      * if they are enabled.\n501:      * <p>\n502:      * Returns early if the timeout expires or if waiting on rejoin is not required\n503:      *\n504:      * @param timer Timer bounding how long this method can block\n505:      * @param waitForJoinGroup Boolean flag indicating if we should wait until re-join group completes\n506:      * @throws KafkaException if the rebalance callback throws an exception\n507:      * @return true iff the operation succeeded\n508:      */\n509:     public boolean poll(Timer timer, boolean waitForJoinGroup) {\n510:         maybeUpdateSubscriptionMetadata();\n511: \n512:         invokeCompletedOffsetCommitCallbacks();\n513: \n514:         if (subscriptions.hasAutoAssignedPartitions()) {\n515:             if (protocol == null) {\n516:                 throw new IllegalStateException(\"User configured \" + ConsumerConfig.PARTITION_ASSIGNMENT_STRATEGY_CONFIG +\n517:                     \" to empty while trying to subscribe for group protocol to auto assign partitions\");\n518:             }\n519:             // Always update the heartbeat last poll time so that the heartbeat thread does not leave the\n520:             // group proactively due to application inactivity even if (say) the coordinator cannot be found.\n521:             pollHeartbeat(timer.currentTimeMs());\n522:             if (coordinatorUnknownAndUnreadySync(timer)) {\n523:                 return false;\n524:             }\n525: \n526:             if (rejoinNeededOrPending()) {\n527:                 // due to a race condition between the initial metadata fetch and the initial rebalance,\n528:                 // we need to ensure that the metadata is fresh before joining initially. This ensures\n529:                 // that we have matched the pattern against the cluster's topics at least once before joining.\n530:                 if (subscriptions.hasPatternSubscription()) {\n531:                     // For consumer group that uses pattern-based subscription, after a topic is created,\n532:                     // any consumer that discovers the topic after metadata refresh can trigger rebalance\n533:                     // across the entire consumer group. Multiple rebalances can be triggered after one topic\n534:                     // creation if consumers refresh metadata at vastly different times. We can significantly\n535:                     // reduce the number of rebalances caused by single topic creation by asking consumer to\n536:                     // refresh metadata before re-joining the group as long as the refresh backoff time has\n537:                     // passed.\n538:                     if (this.metadata.timeToAllowUpdate(timer.currentTimeMs()) == 0) {\n539:                         this.metadata.requestUpdate(true);\n540:                     }\n541: \n542:                     if (!client.ensureFreshMetadata(timer)) {\n543:                         return false;\n544:                     }\n545: \n546:                     maybeUpdateSubscriptionMetadata();\n547:                 }\n548: \n549:                 // if not wait for join group, we would just use a timer of 0\n550:                 if (!ensureActiveGroup(waitForJoinGroup ? timer : time.timer(0L))) {\n551:                     // since we may use a different timer in the callee, we'd still need\n552:                     // to update the original timer's current time after the call\n553:                     timer.update(time.milliseconds());\n554: \n555:                     return false;\n556:                 }\n557:             }\n558:         } else {\n559:             // For manually assigned partitions, we do not try to pro-actively lookup coordinator;\n560:             // instead we only try to refresh metadata when necessary.\n561:             // If connections to all nodes fail, wakeups triggered while attempting to send fetch\n562:             // requests result in polls returning immediately, causing a tight loop of polls. assignments returned by the assignor such that no owned partitions are going to\n718:      * be reassigned to a different consumer directly: if the assignor wants to reassign an owned partition,\n719:      * it must first remove it from the new assignment of the current owner so that it is not assigned to any\n720:      * member, and then in the next rebalance it can finally reassign those partitions not owned by anyone to consumers.\n721:      */\n722:     private void validateCooperativeAssignment(final Map<String, List<TopicPartition>> ownedPartitions,\n723:                                                final Map<String, Assignment> assignments) {\n724:         Set<TopicPartition> totalRevokedPartitions = new HashSet<>();\n725:         SortedSet<TopicPartition> entry.getValue();\n728:             final Set<TopicPartition> addedPartitions = new HashSet<>(assignment.partitions());\n729:             addedPartitions.removeAll(ownedPartitions.get(entry.getKey()));\n730:             final Set<TopicPartition> revokedPartitions = new HashSet<>(ownedPartitions.get(entry.getKey()));\n731:      \"by some members\", totalAddedPartitions);\n744: \n745:             throw new IllegalStateException(\"Assignor supporting the COOPERATIVE protocol violates its requirements\");\n746:         }\n747:     }\n748: \n749:     @Override\n750:     protected boolean onJoinPrepare(Timer timer, int generation, String memberId) {\n751:         log.debug(\"Executing onJoinPrepare with generation {} // owned partitions would be lost, we should trigger the callback and cleanup the assignment;\n807:         // otherwise we can proceed normally and revoke the partitions depending on the private void maybeMarkPartitionsPendingRevocation() {\n865:         if (protocol != RebalanceProtocol.EAGER) {\n866:             return;\n867:         }\n868: \n869:         // When asynchronously @Override\n913:     public boolean rejoinNeededOrPending() {\n914:         if (!subscriptions.hasAutoAssignedPartitions())\n915:             return false;\n916: \n917:         // we need to rejoin if                            final Timer timer) {\n963:         if (partitions.isEmpty()) return Collections.emptyMap();\n964: \n965:         final Generation generationForOffsetRequest = callback) {\n1047:         invokeCompletedOffsetCommitCallbacks();\n1048: \n1049:         RequestFuture<Void> future = null;\n1050:         if (offsets.isEmpty()) {\n1051:             // No need to
